create or replace PROCEDURE  "BRF68_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 

  v_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY');


BEGIN

INSERT INTO BRF68_MAPPING_TABLE
(CUST_ID,FORACID,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,BACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,
HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,REPORT_DATE,GENDER,NATIONALITY,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,NRE_STATUS)

SELECT CUST_ID,ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,BACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,
CONSTITUTION_CODE,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,REPORT_DATE,GENDER,NATIONALITY,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,NRE_FLG FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE
WHERE
    report_date = '30-JUN-2023';
    
    
INSERT INTO BRF68_MAPPING_TABLE (FORACID, ACCT_NAME, ACCT_CRNCY_CODE, REPORT_DATE, ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC)
SELECT ACCT_NO, ACCT_NAME, CURRENCY, REPORT_DATE, AMT_LC
FROM BRF_TREASURY_MASTER_TB
WHERE REPORT_DATE = '30-JUN-2023' ;
COMMIT;

--NON -RESIDENT
UPDATE BRF68_MAPPING_TABLE 
SET NRE_STATUS = 'Y' 
WHERE report_date = '30-JUN-2023' 
AND schm_code IN ('CA108', 'SB102', 'TD105', 'TD106');
COMMIT;
--RESIDENT
UPDATE BRF68_MAPPING_TABLE 
SET NRE_STATUS = 'N'

AND NVL(schm_code,0) NOT IN ('CA108', 'SB102', 'TD105', 'TD106');

create or replace PROCEDURE BRF68_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 

BEGIN


--delete from BRF68_DETAILTABLE where REPORT_DATE = V_REPORT_DATE;
--Commit;

INSERT INTO BRF68_DETAILTABLE
(CUST_ID,FORACID,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,BACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,
HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,REPORT_DATE,GENDER,NATIONALITY,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,NRE_STATUS)

SELECT CUST_ID,ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,GL_CODE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,SOL_ID,ACID,BACID,LEGAL_ENTITY_TYPE,
CONSTITUTION_CODE,HNI_NETWORTH,TURNOVER,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,COUNTRY,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,REPORT_DATE,GENDER,NATIONALITY,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,NRE_FLG FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE
WHERE
    report_date = '30-JUN-2023';
    
    
INSERT INTO BRF68_DETAILTABLE (FORACID, ACCT_NAME, ACCT_CRNCY_CODE, REPORT_DATE, ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC)
SELECT ACCT_NO, ACCT_NAME, CURRENCY, REPORT_DATE, AMT_LC
FROM BRF_TREASURY_MASTER_TB
WHERE REPORT_DATE = '30-JUN-2023' ;
COMMIT;

MERGE INTO BRF68_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT DISTINCT b.REPORT_LABEL_1, b.cust_id, b.foracid, b.REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1, b.REPORT_NAME_1
    FROM BRF68_MAPPING_TABLE b
    JOIN BRF68_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = '30-JUN-2023'
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.REPORT_LABEL_1 = S.REPORT_LABEL_1,
    M.REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1 = S.REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,
    M.REPORT_NAME_1 = S.REPORT_NAME_1
WHERE M.report_date = '30-JUN-2023';

COMMIT;

DELETE FROM brf68_detailtable WHERE REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NULL AND REPORT_NAME_1 IS NULL;
COMMIT;

COMMIT;
END;
